<script data-cfasync="false" src="/cdn-cgi/scripts/5c5dd728/cloudflare-static/email-decode.min.js"></script><script type="text/javascript">
jQuery(document).ready(function(){
    let isHovering = false;

    // When mouse enters either the menu item or mega menu
    jQuery("li#menu-item-55140, .mega-menu-wrap").on("mouseenter", function() {
        isHovering = true;
        jQuery(".mega-menu-wrap").removeClass("hidemenu");
    });

    // When mouse leaves both elements
    jQuery("li#menu-item-55140, .mega-menu-wrap").on("mouseleave", function() {
        isHovering = false;
        setTimeout(function() {
            if (!isHovering) {
                jQuery(".mega-menu-wrap").addClass("hidemenu");
            }
        }, 100); // Small delay for smooth behavior
    });
});

</script>

    function previewImages() {
      xOffset = 200;
      yOffset = 80;
      jQuery(".screenshot").hover(function(e) {
        var windowdiv = jQuery(window).width();
        var htmldiv = jQuery(".mouseOver_text").width();
        var screendiv = jQuery(".screenshot").width();
        var getnewwidth = windowdiv - htmldiv;
        var getnewwidth1 = getnewwidth/2
        var getnewwidth2 = screendiv + getnewwidth1 - 250;

          var $this = jQuery(this); // caching jQuery(this)
          $this.data('initialText', $this.text());
          //$this.text("Download").delay(1200); // Set text
          jQuery("body").append("<div id='previewImage'><img src='" + this.rel + "' alt='rens preview image' />" + "</div>");
          jQuery("#previewImage")
            .css("top", (e.pageY - xOffset) + "px")
            .css("right", (getnewwidth2) + "px")
            .fadeIn("fast");
        },
        function() {
          jQuery("#previewImage").remove();
        });

        jQuery("#previewImage").css("top", (e.pageY - xOffset) + "px");    
      });
    };

document.addEventListener('wpcf7submit', function(event) {
    let form = jQuery(event.target);
    let URL = "https://www.ikf.co.in/zoho/validdata.php";
    var formData = form.serialize();
    jQuery.ajax({
        type: "POST",
        url: URL,
        data: formData,
        success: function(response) {
            console.log(response);
            try {
                const responseObject = JSON.parse(response);
                if (responseObject.status_code == 200) {
                    // window.location.href = 'https://www.ikf.co.in/thank-you/';
                }
            } catch (e) {
                console.error("JSON parse error:", e);
            }
        },
        error: function(xhr, status, error) {
            console.error(error);
        }
    });
}, false);
</script>

			<script>
				const lazyloadRunObserver = () => {
					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});
					}, { rootMargin: '200px 0px 200px 0px' } );
					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {

	jQuery(document).ready(function($){
		// on focus
		jQuery(".wpcf7-form input, .wpcf7-form textarea").focus(function() {
			jQuery(this).parent().siblings('label').addClass('has-value');
		})
		// blur input fields on unfocus + if has no value
			.blur(function() {
			var text_val = jQuery(this).val();
			if(text_val === "") {
				jQuery(this).parent().siblings('label').removeClass('has-value');
			}
		});
	});   
	
	/******** Start header after scrollback ************/
	const body = document.body;
	const scrollUp = "scroll-up";
	const scrollDown = "scroll-down";
	let lastScroll = 0;

	window.addEventListener("scroll", () => {
		const currentScroll = window.pageYOffset;
		if (currentScroll <= 0) {
			body.classList.remove(scrollUp);
			return;
		}
		if (currentScroll > lastScroll && !body.classList.contains(scrollDown)) {
			body.classList.remove(scrollUp);
			body.classList.add(scrollDown);
		} else if (
			currentScroll < lastScroll &&
			body.classList.contains(scrollDown)
		) {
			body.classList.remove(scrollDown);
			body.classList.add(scrollUp);
		}
		lastScroll = currentScroll;
	});
	/******** End header after scrollback ************/ 

	// file upload error

	function changeme(names){ 
		// alert(names)
		var l = jQuery(`select[name='${names}']`).val();
		// alert(l)
		if(l == "" ){
			jQuery('.positions').next().html('<span class="wpcf7-not-valid-tip" aria-hidden="true">Please fill out this field.</span>');    
			jQuery(`select[name='${names}']`).next('.wpcf7-not-valid-tip').show();
		}else{
			jQuery(`select[name='${names}']`).next('.wpcf7-not-valid-tip').hide();

		} 
	}

/* CAREER FORM JS */
jQuery(".remove_up_file").hide();
jQuery("input[name='UploadResume']").change(function() {
	
  let file = jQuery(this)[0].files[0];
  if (file) {
    let fileSizeInMB = Math.ceil(file.size / 1024 / 1024);
    if(fileSizeInMB > 5 ){
      jQuery(".allow-file-size").text(" Your file size: "+fileSizeInMB + " MB").addClass('file_error');
      jQuery(".remove_up_file").show();
    }else{		
      jQuery(".allow-file-size").text(" Your file size: "+fileSizeInMB + " MB").removeClass('file_error');
      jQuery(".remove_up_file").show();
    }    
    jQuery(".allow-file-size").show();
  }
});
jQuery(".remove_up_file").click(function(){ 
        jQuery(this).parent().prev('.uploadFile').find('.filename').text('Upload Resume*'); 
        jQuery(this).parent().prev('.uploadFile').find('input[name="UploadResume"]').val('');
        jQuery(".allow-file-size").hide().removeClass('file_error');
        jQuery(this).hide();
});

<script>
jQuery(window).on('scroll', function () {
    jQuery('.telephony_effect').each(function () {
        var section = jQuery(this);
        var sectionTop = section.offset().top;
        var sectionHeight = section.outerHeight();
        var sectionBottom = sectionTop + sectionHeight;

        var viewportTop = jQuery(window).scrollTop();
        var viewportBottom = viewportTop + jQuery(window).height();

        // Calculate how much of the section is visible
        var visibleTop = Math.max(sectionTop, viewportTop);
        var visibleBottom = Math.min(sectionBottom, viewportBottom);
        var visibleHeight = visibleBottom - visibleTop;

        // Trigger class if 40% or more of the section is visible
        if (visibleHeight > 0 && visibleHeight >= sectionHeight * 0.4) {
            section.addClass('telephony_effect_active');
        } 
    });
});

</script>
<script >

jQuery('.onlycharallow').attr('onkeypress','return validateChar(event)'); 
jQuery('.onlynumallow').attr('onkeypress','return validateNum(event)');

	function validateChar(evt) {
		var charCode = (evt.which) ? evt.which : evt.keyCode;
		if ((charCode < 65 || charCode > 90) && (charCode < 97 || charCode > 123)) {
			if (charCode == 8 || charCode == 32 || charCode == 9)
				return true;
			else
				return false;
		} else
			return true;
	}

	function validateNum(evt) {
		var charCode = (evt.which) ? evt.which : event.keyCode;
		if (charCode > 31 && (charCode < 48 || charCode > 57)) {
			if (charCode == 43 || charCode == 40 || charCode == 41 || charCode == 9)
				return true;
			else
				return false;
		} else
			return true;
	}

	
	// getmessage count
function getMsgCount(this1,cls,messageEle,maxlen,vlue){ 
  // jQuery(".counter").show();  
  jQuery("."+vlue).show();

  // jQuery(".frmcounter").show(); 

  
  var crrlen = parseInt(maxlen);  
  newmsgcount = messageEle.length 
  ans = crrlen-newmsgcount  
  if(ans >= 0){
    
    if(ans === 0 ){
      jQuery(this1).parent().next().text(ans+"/"+crrlen);  
    }else{
      jQuery(this1).parent().next().text(ans+" Characters remaining /"+crrlen);  
    }
    if(ans === 0 ){     
      jQuery(this1).parent().next().addClass('lenend');     
    }else{    
    jQuery(this1).parent().next().removeClass('lenend');
    }    
  }
}

	
jQuery(document).ready(function(){ 

  jQuery(".wpcf7-textarea").attr('oninput','getMsgCount(this,this.name,this.value,jQuery(this).attr("maxlength"), jQuery(this).parent().next().attr("class"))');

});


</script>
